(ALECO) took the opportune time to celebrate the vital role women play in environmental conservation efforts worldwide through a coastal clean-up activity in the coastal barangay of Buhatan, Rapu-Rapu Albay last March 8, 2024.\n\nMore than 30 women residents of the said barangay took part in the activity, which is part of ALECO's Corporate Social Responsibility (CSR), and not only helps to preserve marine ecosystems but also empowers women by providing opportunities for leadership, skill development, and community involvement.\n\nFurthermore, this coastal clean-up action not only recognizes women's efforts to environmental conservation, but also raises their voices and promotes gender equality. ALECO's goal is to encourage and amplify women's voices in environmental preservation, bringing us closer to a more equitable and sustainable future for all.\n\n\xf0\x9d\x91\xaf\xf0\x9d\x92\x82\xf0\x9d\x92\x91\xf0\x9d\x92\x91\xf0\x9d\x92\x9a \xf0\x9d\x91\xbe\xf0\x9d\x92\x90\xf0\x9d\x92\x8e\xf0\x9d\x92\x86\xf0\x9d\x92\x8f\xe2\x80\x99\xf0\x9d\x92\x94 \xf0\x9d\x91\xb4\xf0\x9d\x92\x90\xf0\x9d\x92\x8f\xf0\x9d\x92\x95\xf0\x9d\x92\x89 \xf0\x9d\x91\xaa\xf0\x9d\x92\x86\xf0\x9d\x92\x8d\xf0\x9d\x92\x86\xf0\x9d\x92\x83\xf0\x9d\x92\x93\xf0\x9d\x92\x82\xf0\x9d\x92\x95\xf0\x9d\x92\x8a\xf0\x9d\x92\x90\xf0\x9d\x92\x8f, \xf0\x9d\x92\x8c\xf0\x9d\x92\x82-\xf0\x9d\x91\xa8\xf0\x9d\x91\xb3\xf0\x9d\x91\xac\xf0\x9d\x91\xaa\xf0\x9d\x91\xb6!"

\xf0\x9d\x90\x80\xf0\x9d\x90\x8b\xf0\x9d\x90\x81\xf0\x9d\x90\x80\xf0\x9d\x90\x98 \n\nFollowing decades of living without elctricity, the residents of barangays Buhatan and Galicia saw a glimmer of hope when the committed team from ALECO paid a visit to the island municipality of Rapu-Rapu, Albay on March 7-8, 2024.\n\nAs part of the National Electrification Administration's key projects, ALECO launched an Information and Education Campaign (IEC) on its Sitio Electrification Program (SEP) and Solar Home System (SHS), in keeping with its constant commitment to connect and serve Albayanos.\n\nBy providing funding for the construction of distribution lines and house wiring facilities to qualified households through SEP and the provision of electricity service to dispersed households where distribution lines are either physically or technically unviable for extension through a stand-alone solar home system (SHS), ALECO hopes to achieve 100% electrification of the aforementioned barangays.\n\nThe residents of both Brgy. Buhatan headed by Barangay Captain Ruel \xe2\x80\x9cGob\xe2\x80\x9d Bonto and Brgy. Galicia headed by Barangay Captain Rey Barrameda expressed their warm gratitude for ALECO in taking pro-active steps in energizing their areas."

b'The Albay Electric Cooperative Inc., (ALECO) headed by Acting General Manager Engr. Wilfredo O. Bucsit and the Local Government Unit (LGU) of Bacacay, Albay thru its Municipal Mayor Hon. Edsel B. Belleza convened this afternoon, March 4, 2024 to discuss matters of power supply among the forty-five (45) households of Barangay 13, specifically its concerns in relation to the recent Notices of Disconnection they received. \n\nMeanwhile, ALECO ensured willingness to provide viable solutions for addressing such concerns.\n\nPresent also during the meeting were ISD Manager Ms. Haysli Lucilo, Mr. Elmer Barja and LGU Bacacay Admin Aide Jane Bermas.'
b'\xf0\x9d\x97\x94\xf0\x9d\x97\x9f\xf0\x9d\x97\x98\xf0\x9d\x97\x96\xf0\x9d\x97\xa2 \xf0\x9d\x97\x96\xf0\x9d\x97\xa2\xf0\x9d\x97\xa1\xf0\x9d\x97\x97\xf0\x9d\x97\xa8\xf0\x9d\x97\x96\xf0\x9d\x97\xa7\xf0\x9d\x97\xa6 \xf0\x9d\x97\x94 \xf0\x9d\x97\x96\xf0\x9d\x97\xa2\xf0\x9d\x97\xa1\xf0\x9d\x97\xa7\xf0\x9d\x97\x9c\xf0\x9d\x97\xa1\xf0\x9d\x97\xa8\xf0\x9d\x97\xa2\xf0\x9d\x97\xa8\xf0\x9d\x97\xa6 \xf0\x9d\x97\x94\xf0\x9d\x97\xa3\xf0\x9d\x97\xa3\xf0\x9d\x97\xa5\xf0\x9d\x97\x98\xf0\x9d\x97\x9b\xf0\x9d\x97\x98\xf0\x9d\x97\xa1\xf0\x9d\x97\xa6\xf0\x9d\x97\x9c\xf0\x9d\x97\xa2\xf0\x9d\x97\xa1 \xf0\x9d\x97\x94\xf0\x9d\x97\x96\xf0\x9d\x97\xa7\xf0\x9d\x97\x9c\xf0\x9d\x97\xa9\xf0\x9d\x97\x9c\xf0\x9d\x97\xa7\xf0\x9d\x97\xac \xf0\x9d\x97\x94\xf0\x9d\x97\x9a\xf0\x9d\x97\x94\xf0\x9d\x97\x9c\xf0\x9d\x97\xa1\xf0\x9d\x97\xa6\xf0\x9d\x97\xa7 \xf0\x9d\x97\xa5\xf0\x9d\x97\x94 \xf0\x9d\x97\xa1\xf0\x9d\x97\xa2. \xf0\x9d\x9f\xb3\xf0\x9d\x9f\xb4\xf0\x9d\x9f\xaf\xf0\x9d\x9f\xae \xf0\x9d\x97\xa9\xf0\x9d\x97\x9c\xf0\x9d\x97\xa2\xf0\x9d\x97\x9f\xf0\x9d\x97\x94\xf0\x9d\x97\xa7\xf0\x9d\x97\xa2\xf0\x9d\x97\xa5\xf0\x9d\x97\xa6 \xf0\x9d\x97\x9c\xf0\x9d\x97\xa1 \xf0\x9d\x97\xa7\xf0\x9d\x97\x94\xf0\x9d\x97\x95\xf0\x9d\x97\x94\xf0\x9d\x97\x96\xf0\x9d\x97\xa2 \xf0\x9d\x97\x96\xf0\x9d\x97\x9c\xf0\x9d\x97\xa7\xf0\x9d\x97\xac\n\nThe dedicated team of ALECO, together with some personnel from the media and the National Bureau of Investigation (NBI) conducted a successful anti-pilferage apprehension activity last Friday, March 1, 2024 in the barangays of Bombon, Bangkilingan, Panal and Divino Rostro in Tabaco City.\n\nFour (4) individuals were apprehended for direct tapping violation and one (1) member-consumer for having four disconnected accounts but maintained a power supply and was engaged in illegal reconnection. Another member-consumer was apprehended for violating the law twice due to direct tapping and illegal reconnection and one (1) was issued a subpoena by the NBI.   \n\nALECO is committed to the strict implementation of RA 7832, also known as the Anti-Pilferage Act of 1994. We will not tolerate such violations because it results in the system loss issues of the cooperative, which affects legitimate member consumers.'

Bongalon and Pe\xc3\xb1afrancia, Daraga Albay and Brgy. Estanza, Legazpi City.\n\nTwo member-consumers were apprehended for using unregistered meters, while one member-consumer was apprehended for having a disconnected account but having continued power supply and engaging in illicit reconnection. ALECO has taken the necessary actions against these individuals for violating the Anti-Pilferage Act of 1994, also known as Republic Act No. 7832.\n\nALECO will not tolerate such violations as it leads to the cooperative's system loss issues which in turn affects legitimate member-consumers because of additional costs associated with system loss, issues with power quality, and inefficiencies in the distribution lines, which will lower the dependability of the service."

It stops excessive electric currents during short circuits or overloads, while keeping other circuits running. Switchgear also isolates circuits from power sources and allows multiple sources to power a single load, which helps keep systems running smoothly.\n\nWe apologize for any inconvenience this may have caused and appreciate your understanding, ka-ALECO.'

Consequently, residents of Sitio Barayong, located within Barangay Mariawa, were disconnected from BAPA Talahib, resulting in the de-energization of the entire sitio.\n\nFacing this challenge, residents of Sitio Barayong reached out to ALECO seeking assistance in restoring their electricity supply. Responding to their request, Albay Electric Cooperative, Inc. (ALECO), stipulated that residents must fulfill the necessary documentation requirements within the month.\n\nAfter careful consideration and proper coordination, ALECO decided to energized Sitio Barayong prior to the scheduled date.'

(ALECO) carried out a member clustering activity earlier today in Brgy. Tuliw, Malinao Albay through its personnel from the Technical Services Department (TSD).\n\nThe purpose of this is to ensure that consumers are provided with an accurate reading of their electricity use, as ALECO has replaced its previous meters with modular socket meters. In addition, it is an initiative to identify problems like equipment failures, unathourized use, or meter tampering in order to reduce system losses.\n\nThe initiative's overall goals are to increase operational effectiveness, better service delivery, and make it easier for member consumers to strategically address their complaints about electricity.\n\nALECO will continue this activity until we are able to fully saturate every barangay in the province of Albay for the abovemention objective."

b'A two-batch Seminar-Workshop titled "Meter Reading, Billing, Collection, and Disconnection Enhancement" took place at the ALECO Social Hall on February 12-13 and February 14-15, featuring speakers from the National Electrification Administration (NEA) and attendees from CASURECO II, CASURECO III, and ALECO.\n\nThe event aimed to assess the meter\'s efficiency in reading kWh consumption and to educate participants on the implications of accurate/inaccurate meter readings for the electric cooperative\'s operational effectiveness.\n\nMoreover, the seminar emphasized the importance of staying updated on customer service standards, empowering participants to handle consumer complaints with greater effectiveness and efficiency. Additionally, by making use of the Electric Cooperative\'s available resources\xe2\x80\x94including materials, tools, and personnel\xe2\x80\x94participants were expected to contribute to reducing system loss.'

b"On February 1, 2024, NEA Administrator Antonio Mariano Almeda visited Albay for several days to conduct a consultative meeting with the members of the Bicol Electric Cooperative Association (BECA) to discuss various electrification issues. He also visited several electric cooperatives to check their operational and performance status.\n\nThe consultative meeting discussion revolved around the review of subsidy liquidation, implementation of the Sitio Electrification Program (SEP), and the evaluation of the status of the lifeline rate subsidy program of each Electric Cooperative.\n\nThe meeting was held at the Oriental Hotel and was attended by all BECA members, Albay Electric Cooperative (ALECO), Camarines Sur Electric Cooperatives comprising CASURECO I, II, III, and IV, Camarines Norte Electric Cooperative (CANORECO), First Catanduanes Electric Cooperative (CANORECO), Masbate Electric Cooperative (MASELCO), Sorsogon Electric Cooperatives composed of SORECO I, II, and Ticao Island Electric Cooperative (TISELCO). Also present were NEA representatives, including NEA Deputy Administrator - Atty. Rossan Rosero-Lee (Legal Services and Concurrent MASELCO - Project Supervisor), Atty. Omar Mayo (EC Management Services), Engr. Ernesto Silvano Jr. (Technical Services), Corporate Secretary Atty. Gwen Enciso-Kyamko, and Corporate Communication and Social Marketing Office Department Manager Atty. Emil Cuyugan.\n\nDuring the discussion, NEA Administrator Almeda ensured that all electric cooperatives' issues were resolved and that they were able to meet the NEA Program's requirements to support both government demands and stakeholders needs handled by each electric cooperative."

b"JUST NOW, Albay Electric Cooperative, Inc. (ALECO), held a meeting with the Liga ng Barangay of Malinao to discuss ways to strengthen community ties. The primary focus was on improving communication channels to ensure that important information about power interruptions, changes in power rates, and other relevant activities reaches residents efficiently. A key aspect of this plan is to establish a comprehensive barangay network information campaign initiated by the Member Services Division. \n\nALECO strongly believes that enhancing this campaign will not only build trust among its consumers but also promote transparency regarding the cooperative's efforts to benefit the Albayano community. By keeping stakeholders well-informed, ALECO aims to foster a sense of shared responsibility and unity, thereby improving its relationship with the community.\n\nMoreover, ALECO sees collaborative partnerships with barangay officials, local organizations, and schools as essential for expanding the reach of its information dissemination efforts. By leveraging the networks and resources of these entities, ALECO intends to overcome communication barriers and ensure that even remote areas receive important updates. Through working together with these valued partners, ALECO hopes to encourage proactive involvement from every member of the community in shaping the cooperative's journey towards progress and prosperity.\n\n#ALECOCommunityConnect \xe2\x80\xa2 #ALECOnnect \xe2\x80\xa2 #ALECOCommunityTies \xe2\x80\xa2 #BarangayNetworkCampaign\n#CommunityEmpowerment #EmpoweringCommunities"

b'FOR IMMEDIATE RELEASE\nALECO ADDRESSES POWER OUTAGE IN KAWIT EAST WASHINGTON AND ILAWOD ALBAY\n\nLegazpi City, Albay \xe2\x80\x93 January 10, 2024 \xe2\x80\x93 Albay Electric Cooperative, Inc. (ALECO) informs its valued consumers of a power outage affecting portions of Purok 2, Brgy. 16 Kawit East Washington near Castillo Homes and parts of Brgy. 17, Ilawod Albay near the railway. The outage is due to a busted 50 KVA domestic transformer.\n\nALECO\xe2\x80\x99s Technical Services Department is currently mobilizing personnel and equipment to address the issue. The team is targeting to replace the transformer within this day, January 10, 2024.\nALECO apologizes for any disruption to daily routines and business operations caused by this unexpected outage. We will provide updates on the restoration process through our official social media pages.\nAffected consumers are advised to take necessary precautions, such as unplugging appliances and electronics to prevent damage upon power restoration.\n\nALECO remains committed to providing reliable and efficient electric service to its consumers. We appreciate your patience and understanding as we work to resolve this issue.'

(ALECO) fulfilled their longstanding dream of connection to the power grid. After four years of living without electricity, a brighter future shines for these villagers thanks to ALECO's dedicated efforts.\n\nThis heartwarming initiative kicked off on December 28, 2023, with ALECO staff bringing warm smiles and much-needed relief to the community. Before the power lines were switched on, families received essential food and school supplies, spreading joy among the children and adults alike.\n\nThis project embodies ALECO's unwavering commitment to bringing safe and reliable electricity to every corner of Albay. \n\nA few years back, these families are connected through Barangay Power Association (BAPA) \xe2\x80\x93 ALECO's dedicated arm focused on enhancing service efficiency and community upliftment \xe2\x80\x93 adds another layer of empowerment. BAPA facilitates efficient service delivery, reduces system losses, and encourages community participation in cooperative programs. By complying to the requirements and settling BAPA arrears, residents gain individual connections with ALECO.\n\nThis initiative goes beyond providing light; it ignites a flame of self-reliance and community responsibility. ALECO's commitment to illuminating dreams across Albay continues, one Sitio Bonglas at a time."

(ALECO) marked a significant milestone today with the successful retrieval of its two reclosers from the National Grid Corporation of the Philippines (NGCP) substation in Sto. Domingo, Albay. These vital pieces of equipment, responsible for Sta. Misericordia Feeder 1 and 2, are now under ALECO's direct management, promising a brighter future for its member-consumers.\n\nThe relocation, completed swiftly on December 21st, unlocks a multitude of benefits for Albay's power infrastructure. This include enhanced reliability by bringing the reclosers closer to home, ALECO gains faster access for maintenance and repairs, minimizing downtime and ensuring smoother power flow.\n\nThis initiative will also mitigate power outages. The ability to swiftly address faults and trip-offs translates to fewer and shorter power interruptions for residents under these feeders. Faster maintenance translates to quicker resolution of power supply concerns, ensuring member-consumers receive prompt and efficient service.\n\nThe resource allocation will also be optimized because the relocation reduces the need for manpower stationed within the NGCP compound, allowing ALECO to allocate resources more effectively.\n\nRelocating the reclosers outside the NGCP compound mitigates the risk of potential incidents within the substation, promoting overall safety for all parties involved.\n\nEasier access to the reclosers allows ALECO's response teams to act swiftly in case of trip-offs caused by vegetation or other external factors.\n\nThis bold step towards greater control symbolizes ALECO's commitment to continuous improvement and unwavering dedication to its member-consumers. The proactive retrieval of the reclosers, coupled with ongoing massive clearing efforts, paves the way for a more dependable and resilient power system for the province.\n\nWith this initiative, ALECO reaffirms its position as a leading force in Albay's energy landscape, consistently prioritizing the needs and well-being of its member-consumers. The successful relocation of the reclosers marks a turning point, ushering in a new era of reliable and efficient power distribution for the province.\n\n#ALECOPressRelease #ALECOnnect"

b'Albay Electric Cooperative Inc. (ALECO) is aware of the power line damage that occurred in certain areas of Zone 3, Bitano, Legazpi City yesterday, December 19, 2023, in relation to a test run conducted by the Philippine National Railways.\n\nWe understand the inconvenience this has caused affected residents and businesses. ALECO immediately dispatched crews to assess the situation and begin restoration efforts. As of this update, we are still actively working to restore power to all affected areas. Our priority is to isolate the damaged lines to prevent further service disruptions.\nInitial reports indicate that some internet cables were also affected in the incident. \n\nALECO has mobilized additional equipment and personnel to address any other related damage that may be discovered in neighboring areas. We are committed to restoring full power and minimizing any inconvenience caused by this unexpected event.\n\nWe will continue to provide updates on the progress of restoration efforts through our official channels, including our social media platforms. Residents are encouraged to contact ALECO customer service for any inquiries or concerns.\n\nWe appreciate your patience and understanding as we work diligently to restore normalcy.'

b"\xf0\x9d\x90\x80\xf0\x9d\x90\x8b\xf0\x9d\x90\x81\xf0\x9d\x90\x80\xf0\x9d\x90\x98 \xf0\x9d\x90\x84\xf0\x9d\x90\x8b\xf0\x9d\x90\x84\xf0\x9d\x90\x82\xf0\x9d\x90\x93\xf0\x9d\x90\x91\xf0\x9d\x90\x88\xf0\x9d\x90\x82 \xf0\x9d\x90\x82\xf0\x9d\x90\x8e\xf0\x9d\x90\x8e\xf0\x9d\x90\x8f\xf0\x9d\x90\x84\xf0\x9d\x90\x91\xf0\x9d\x90\x80\xf0\x9d\x90\x93\xf0\x9d\x90\x88\xf0\x9d\x90\x95\xf0\x9d\x90\x84 \xf0\x9d\x90\x88\xf0\x9d\x90\x8d\xf0\x9d\x90\x82. (\xf0\x9d\x90\x80\xf0\x9d\x90\x8b\xf0\x9d\x90\x84\xf0\x9d\x90\x82\xf0\x9d\x90\x8e) \xf0\x9d\x90\x92\xf0\x9d\x90\x93\xf0\x9d\x90\x91\xf0\x9d\x90\x84\xf0\x9d\x90\x8d\xf0\x9d\x90\x86\xf0\x9d\x90\x93\xf0\x9d\x90\x87\xf0\x9d\x90\x84\xf0\x9d\x90\x8d\xf0\x9d\x90\x92 \xf0\x9d\x90\x84\xf0\x9d\x90\x8c\xf0\x9d\x90\x84\xf0\x9d\x90\x91\xf0\x9d\x90\x86\xf0\x9d\x90\x84\xf0\x9d\x90\x8d\xf0\x9d\x90\x82\xf0\x9d\x90\x98 \xf0\x9d\x90\x91\xf0\x9d\x90\x84\xf0\x9d\x90\x92\xf0\x9d\x90\x8f\xf0\x9d\x90\x8e\xf0\x9d\x90\x8d\xf0\x9d\x90\x92\xf0\x9d\x90\x84 \xf0\x9d\x90\x82\xf0\x9d\x90\x80\xf0\x9d\x90\x8f\xf0\x9d\x90\x80\xf0\x9d\x90\x81\xf0\x9d\x90\x88\xf0\x9d\x90\x8b\xf0\x9d\x90\x88\xf0\x9d\x90\x93\xf0\x9d\x90\x88\xf0\x9d\x90\x84\xf0\x9d\x90\x92 \xf0\x9d\x90\x93\xf0\x9d\x90\x87\xf0\x9d\x90\x91\xf0\x9d\x90\x8e\xf0\x9d\x90\x94\xf0\x9d\x90\x86\xf0\x9d\x90\x87 \xf0\x9d\x9f\x91-\xf0\x9d\x90\x83\xf0\x9d\x90\x80\xf0\x9d\x90\x98 \xf0\x9d\x90\x81\xf0\x9d\x90\x80\xf0\x9d\x90\x92\xf0\x9d\x90\x88\xf0\x9d\x90\x82 \xf0\x9d\x90\x88\xf0\x9d\x90\x8d\xf0\x9d\x90\x82\xf0\x9d\x90\x88\xf0\x9d\x90\x83\xf0\x9d\x90\x84\xf0\x9d\x90\x8d\xf0\x9d\x90\x93 \xf0\x9d\x90\x82\xf0\x9d\x90\x8e\xf0\x9d\x90\x8c\xf0\x9d\x90\x8c\xf0\x9d\x90\x80\xf0\x9d\x90\x8d\xf0\x9d\x90\x83 \xf0\x9d\x90\x92\xf0\x9d\x90\x98\xf0\x9d\x90\x92\xf0\x9d\x90\x93\xf0\x9d\x90\x84\xf0\x9d\x90\x8c \xf0\x9d\x90\x93\xf0\x9d\x90\x91\xf0\x9d\x90\x80\xf0\x9d\x90\x88\xf0\x9d\x90\x8d\xf0\x9d\x90\x88\xf0\x9d\x90\x8d\xf0\x9d\x90\x86\n\nAlbay Electric Cooperative Inc. (ALECO) takes a proactive step towards enhancing its emergency response capabilities by actively participating in the 3-Day Basic Incident Command System Training. The event, initiated by the Municipality of Daraga and its Municipal Disaster Risk Reduction and Management Council (Daraga-MDRRMO), was held from December 12 to 14, 2023, at Antonia's Restaurant, Cafe, and Events place in Daraga, Albay.\n\nUnder the leadership of Engr. Bim Dineros, the MDRRMC organized the comprehensive training, bringing together various key stakeholders involved in disaster response and management. Participants included representatives from the Philippine Army, Philippine National Police, Bureau of Fire Protection, Philippine Chamber of Commerce, Barangay Health Workers, Civil Society Organizations such as Prime Water and Symon of Cyrene, and various educational institutions.\n\nThe distinguished panel of instructors featured experts in emergency response and disaster management, including Jasper Navarra of Philippine Red Cross - Albay, Ramil Marianito of Philippine Information Agency, PMAJ Kim Arenas of Police Regional Office 5, Peter Andrew Balmaceda of Legazpi City National High School, Mark Anthony Ate of Office of Civil Defense 5, and Gremil Alexis Naz of Office of Civil Defense 5.\n\nThe training covered a range of crucial topics including ICS Organization and Staffing, Facilities, Managing Planned Events and Major Incidents, Incident/Event Assessment and Management by Objectives, Organizing and Managing Incident Resources, Incident and Event Planning, Transfer of Command, Demobilization, and Close-Out.\n\nThe culminating event of the training featured closing remarks from Mr. Jessar B. Adornado, Office of Civil Defense 5 DRRM Division Chief, emphasizing the significance of collaborative efforts in disaster response and management.\nLooking ahead, participants are expected to reconvene next year for the level 2 of the training, further solidifying the knowledge and skills gained during the 3-day intensive program.\n\nThis initiative underscores ALECO's commitment to the safety and well-being of the communities it serves, as well as its dedication to fostering a culture of preparedness and resilience in the face of emergencies."

(ALECO) elections on December 9, 2023.\n\nSaenz received the full support of the voting members in District I (Tiwi and Malinao), while Bordeos garnered unanimous approval from District IV (Legazpi and Rapu-Rapu).\n\nDistricts I and IV conducted elections smoothly; however, the District Election Committee (DECOM) for District VII (Guinobatan, Jovellar, and Pioduran) had previously declared a failure of elections, attributing it to the absence of a duly qualified applicant-candidate to represent the District.\n\nDespite this setback, the successful ALECO District Elections held in Districts I and IV represent a significant step forward in ensuring strong representation for local communities within Albay province. With Saenz and Bordeos at the helm, both districts are well-positioned to thrive in the years ahead.\n\n#ALECO2023DE'
b"ALECO LIGHTS UP WITH ALMOST 5,000 LED CHRISTMAS TREE\n\nAlbay Electric Cooperative, Inc. (ALECO) ushered in the holiday season with a dazzling display of light officially lit its 25-foot Christmas tree.\n\nAlmost 5,000 LED lights adorned the majestic tree, creating a festive spectacle that can be seen from afar. Twelve circular ornament lights further added to its charm and beauty. The Technical Services Department and Building Program Committee, led by Engr. Khein Llaguno, worked tirelessly for three days to bring this vision to life.\n\nAccording to Engr. Llaguno, this Christmas tree represents ALECO's capacity to distribute reliable power supply to its member-consumers.\n\nLinemen, personnel of Institutional Services Division (ISD), and other utility men also played a crucial role in constructing the tree. However, Engr. Llaguno specifically acknowledged the significant contribution of Mr. Andy Rimbao, the cooperative's utility man who built 60% of the tree.\n\nThe Christmas lighting ceremony was followed by a birthday celebration for AGM Engr. Wilfredo O. Bucsit, with a spectacular fireworks display that lit up the night sky.\n\nBefore the official lighting, the grotto of the Blessed Virgin Mary was blessed, providing a space for employees and member-consumers to offer prayers and seek solace during the holiday season.\n\nThis year, ALECO's Christmas tree is not just a festive decoration but also a testament to the cooperative's commitment to providing its member-consumers with reliable and efficient power supply."

b'Sa ika-160 na kaarawan ni Gat Andres Bonifacio, isang matamis na pagpupugay sa bayaning nagbigay-buhay sa diwa ng pakikibaka para sa kalayaan ng Pilipinas. Isinilang noong Nobyembre 30, 1863, si Bonifacio ay naglingkod bilang inspirasyon para sa sambayanan, itinataguyod ang pagkakaisa at pag-aangat ng mga inaapi. Ang kanyang di-matitinag na dedikasyon at katapangan sa harap ng mga hamon ng buhay ay nagpapatuloy na nagbibigay liwanag sa landas ng ating kasaysayan.\n\nSa bawat kaarawan ni Bonifacio, binibigyan natin diin ang kahalagahan ng pagpapahalaga sa ating kasarinlan at pag-unlad ng bansa. Ang kanyang diwa at mga aral ay patuloy na naglalakbay sa puso ng bawat Pilipino, na nagbibigay inspirasyon sa atin na maging tapat sa ating mga pangarap para sa isang malaya at maunlad na bansa. Maligayang kaarawan, Gat Andres Bonifacio! \xf0\x9f\x87\xb5\xf0\x9f\x87\xad\xe2\x9d\xa4\xef\xb8\x8f #Bonifacio160 #Bayani #KasaysayanNgPilipinas'

b'IN PHOTOS | ALECO, together with four representatives from the Energy Regulatory Commission (ERC), held a seminar in the ALECO Boardroom. The session, attended by 34 participants, covered Republic Act 7832, known as "Anti-Electricity and Electric Transmission Lines/Materials Pilferage," and included discussions on Guidelines for Meter Shop Accreditation, as well as In-Service Testing and Validation.\n\nThe ERC representatives\xe2\x80\x94Joevyn V. Peralta, Marvin C. Saccuan, Eman E. Angelitud, and Alvin G. Noveno\xe2\x80\x94reiterated the significance of the seminar in relation to the cooperative. Additionally, they provided insights to enhance and fortify operational processes.\n\nAs part of ALECO\'s mission to provide reliable electricity to Albayanos at fair prices, it is crucial to inform its member-consumer-owners (MCO) that electricity theft significantly contributes to system losses. This directly impacts the rise in power rates and, if left unaddressed, may lead to setbacks for our cooperative.\n\n#StopElectricTheft #SayNoToPowerTheft #AntiElectricityTheft #PowerCrimeAwareness #ElectricityEthics #ReportElectricTheft #PowerTheftAwareness #ElectricalSafetyFirst #EnergyEthics #EndPowerTheft #AntiPilferageAct #RA7832'

(ALECO) is fully prepared to safeguard power supply during the upcoming Barangay and Sangguniang Kabataan Elections 2023 in Albay Province. \n\nTo ensure uninterrupted electricity service, ALECO prepared a comprehensive contingency plan; outlining standard operating procedures that will be implemented before, during, and after the election.\n\nThe primary objective of this plan is to guarantee a seamless power supply during the election period. ALECO's commitment to this mission is highlighted through the following key purposes:\n\n1. Uninterrupted Power Supply. ALECO is dedicated to providing a continuous power supply throughout the election event.\n\n2. Swift Repairs. In the event of damaged distribution lines and equipment, ALECO's task force is prepared to undertake rapid repair and restoration measures.\n\n3. Immediate Restoration. In case of power supply disruptions in polling precincts, ALECO will prioritize immediate restoration to ensure the voting process is unaffected.\n\n4. Safety. ALECO will place the utmost importance on ensuring the safety of all individuals involved in the election process.\n\nTo execute these objectives effectively, ALECO has put in place a series of contingency measures, including readiness of line hardware, materials, and equipment, distribution line facilities, support systems, key personnel, and an Emergency Response Team (ERT). \n\nManpower augmentation and a communication directory have also been integrated into the plan. Deployment of a focal person through the Member Services Division to the COMELEC Command Center for improved communication and rapid response.\n\nWith this comprehensive contingency plan in place, ALECO stands prepared to meet the power needs of the community during this important event.\n\n#alecoasikaso\n#NEAPowerTaskForce\n#2023BSKE\n#WePromisedWeDelivered\n#BSKE2023Election"

cooperative to realize this initiative. b'Sa aming mga Member-Consumer-Owners,\n\xe2\x80\x8b\nNais naming ipaalam na magkakaroon kami ng Disconnection Activity sa ilang lugar. Bilang bahagi ng aming patuloy na pagsusumikap upang matiyak ang patas at mahusay na operasyon, ang mga account na mayroong outstanding bills o arrears ay maaring maputulan.\n\xe2\x80\x8b\nAlinsunod sa aming patakaran at pamamaraan, ang mga account na may outstanding bills o arrears sa loob ng itinalagang takdang panahon ay mapuputulan ng suplay ng kuryente. Ang hakbang na ito ay kinakailangan upang mapanatili ang pinansyal na aspeto ng kooperatiba at mapangalagaan ang interes ng bawat Member-Consumer-Owners.\n\xe2\x80\x8b\nUpang maiwasan ang pagkadiskonekta ng inyong suplay ng kuryente, inirerekomenda naming isaalang-alang ang mga sumusunod na opsyon upang mabayaran ang inyong power bills sa takdang panahon:\n1. \xf0\x9d\x90\x8f\xf0\x9d\x90\x9e\xf0\x9d\x90\xab\xf0\x9d\x90\xac\xf0\x9d\x90\xa8\xf0\x9d\x90\xa7\xf0\x9d\x90\x9a\xf0\x9d\x90\xa5 \xf0\x9d\x90\xa7\xf0\x9d\x90\x9a \xf0\x9d\x90\x8f\xf0\x9d\x90\x9a\xf0\x9d\x90\xa0\xf0\x9d\x90\x9b\xf0\x9d\x90\x9a\xf0\x9d\x90\x9b\xf0\x9d\x90\x9a\xf0\x9d\x90\xb2\xf0\x9d\x90\x9a\xf0\x9d\x90\x9d: Bisitahin ang malapit na ASCO para magbayad. Ang aming mga tauhan ay handang tumulong sa inyo at magbigay ng kinakailangang gabay.\n2. \xf0\x9d\x90\x80\xf0\x9d\x90\x8b\xf0\x9d\x90\x84\xf0\x9d\x90\x82\xf0\x9d\x90\x8e \xf0\x9d\x90\x8f\xf0\x9d\x90\x9a\xf0\x9d\x90\xb2\xf0\x9d\x90\xa6\xf0\x9d\x90\x9e\xf0\x9d\x90\xa7\xf0\x9d\x90\xad \xf0\x9d\x90\x82\xf0\x9d\x90\x9e\xf0\x9d\x90\xa7\xf0\x9d\x90\xad\xf0\x9d\x90\x9e\xf0\x9d\x90\xab\xf0\x9d\x90\xac: Maaring magbayad sa aming mga akreditadong payment centers para sa mabilis na transaksyon.\n\xe2\x80\xa2 Bayad Center\n\xe2\x80\xa2 Camalig Bank\n\xe2\x80\xa2 ECPay\n\xe2\x80\xa2 UnionBank\n\xe2\x80\x8b\nPinapaalala namin na napakahalaga na mabayaran kaagad ang inyong power bills upang maiwasan ang anumang pagkaantala sa inyong suplay ng kuryente. Kapag naputulan, kinakailangan na bayaran ang lahat ng outstanding bills kasama ang bayad para sa pagpapabalik ng serbisyo (reconnection fee).\n\xe2\x80\x8b\nPinahahalagahan namin ang inyong pagiging Member-Consumer-Owners at ang tiwala na inyong ibinigay sa ating kooperatiba. Sa pamamagitan ng pagtutulungan upang mabayaran ang ating power bills sa loob ng takdang panahon, masisiguro natin ang patuloy na maayos at abot-kayang suplay ng kuryente para sa lahat ng mga miyembro ng kooperatiba.\n\xe2\x80\x8b\nMaraming salamat sa inyong atensyon at kooperasyon.\n\xe2\x80\x8b\n\xf0\x9d\x90\x83\xf0\x9d\x90\x84\xf0\x9d\x90\x93\xf0\x9d\x90\x80\xf0\x9d\x90\x88\xf0\x9d\x90\x8b\xf0\x9d\x90\x92 \xf0\x9d\x90\x81\xf0\x9d\x90\x84\xf0\x9d\x90\x8b\xf0\x9d\x90\x8e\xf0\x9d\x90\x96:\xf0\x9f\x94\x8c\n\xe2\x80\x8b\n\xf0\x9d\x90\x83\xf0\x9d\x90\x88\xf0\x9d\x90\x92\xf0\x9d\x90\x82\xf0\x9d\x90\x8e\xf0\x9d\x90\x8d\xf0\x9d\x90\x8d\xf0\x9d\x90\x84\xf0\x9d\x90\x82\xf0\x9d\x90\x93\xf0\x9d\x90\x88\xf0\x9d\x90\x8e\xf0\x9d\x90\x8d \xf0\x9d\x90\x92\xf0\x9d\x90\x82\xf0\x9d\x90\x87\xf0\x9d\x90\x84\xf0\x9d\x90\x83\xf0\x9d\x90\x94\xf0\x9d\x90\x8b\xf0\x9d\x90\x84: OCTOBER 17 - 19 (TUESDAY - THURSDAY)\n\xe2\x80\x8b\n\xf0\x9d\x90\x8e\xf0\x9d\x90\x82\xf0\x9d\x90\x93\xf0\x9d\x90\x8e\xf0\x9d\x90\x81\xf0\x9d\x90\x84\xf0\x9d\x90\x91 \xf0\x9d\x9f\x8f\xf0\x9d\x9f\x95 (\xf0\x9d\x90\x93\xf0\x9d\x90\x94\xf0\x9d\x90\x84\xf0\x9d\x90\x92\xf0\x9d\x90\x83\xf0\x9d\x90\x80\xf0\x9d\x90\x98)\n\xe2\x80\xa2 BACACAY\n\xe2\x80\xa2 CAMALIG\n\xe2\x80\xa2 DARAGA\n\xe2\x80\xa2 LEGAZPI\n\xe2\x80\xa2 LIGAO\n\xe2\x80\xa2 POLANGUI\n\xe2\x80\xa2 STO. b"\xf0\x9d\x90\x93\xf0\x9d\x90\x80\xf0\x9d\x90\x8a\xf0\x9d\x90\x84 \xf0\x9d\x90\x88\xf0\x9d\x90\x93 \xf0\x9d\x90\x84\xf0\x9d\x90\x80\xf0\x9d\x90\x92\xf0\x9d\x90\x98, \xf0\x9d\x90\x8c\xf0\x9d\x90\x86\xf0\x9d\x90\x80 \xf0\x9d\x90\x8a\xf0\x9d\x90\x80\xf0\x9d\x90\x92\xf0\x9d\x90\x80\xf0\x9d\x90\x8c\xf0\x9d\x90\x80 \xf0\x9d\x90\x92\xf0\x9d\x90\x80 \xf0\x9d\x90\x84\xf0\x9d\x90\x82!\n\nIn celebration of both National Cooperative Month and National Mental Health Month this October, ALECO representatives actively participated in the virtual event hosted by the Philippine Rural Electrification Cooperatives Association Inc. (PHILRECA).\n\nOne of the key discussions centered around the importance of establishing a healthy work-life balance. This is a critical consideration not only for individuals employed in Electric Cooperatives but also for anyone facing high demands in their professional or personal life.\n\nRecognizing the significance of mental health and learning ways to enhance it can unlock an individual's full potential. This, in turn, enhances their capacity to fulfill their responsibilities and make valuable contributions to the community. The discussions also covered strategies for managing and coping with stress, providing valuable insights on maintaining overall well-being. \xf0\x9f\x92\x9b\xf0\x9f\x92\x99\n\n\xf0\x9d\x90\x96\xf0\x9d\x90\x80\xf0\x9d\x90\x93\xf0\x9d\x90\x82\xf0\x9d\x90\x87 \xf0\x9d\x90\x85\xf0\x9d\x90\x94\xf0\x9d\x90\x8b\xf0\x9d\x90\x8b \xf0\x9d\x90\x95\xf0\x9d\x90\x88\xf0\x9d\x90\x83\xf0\x9d\x90\x84\xf0\x9d\x90\x8e:\nhttps://www.facebook.com/PHILRECA.INC/videos/981909922923870\n\n#TakeItEasyYear3\n#MentalHealthMatters\n#ALECOCares\n#PHILRECA \n#TakeItEasyMgaKasamaSaEC\n#PowerOn\n#OneECMCOMovement #SaPHILRECAProtektadoKa"

b'From NGCP: Cause of Power Interruption impacting POLANGUI Substation'
b"Today | At the Sangguniang Panglungsod Session Hall in Legazpi City, ALECO representatives Ms. Luna Gracia Mayor-Reodique, Mr. Jonathan Sadueste, and Mr. Manduriao met with DPWH 2nd Engineering Office led by Engr. Agnes Padua to discuss an infrastructure project. The focus was on energizing a two-storey multi-purpose building in Baranggay 58-Buraguis, Legazpi City.\n\nALECO, while fully supportive of government projects, emphasized the importance of adhering to the correct procedures. Furthermore, ALECO is aware of the potential community consequences if the facility is energized without its dedicated transformer.\n\nAs the meeting progressed, both parties reached an agreement to realign the electrical plan and associated documents to meet ALECO's requirements for electrification.\n\n#InfrastructureDevelopment\n#ALECOSupportGovernment\n#GovernmentPartnership\n#ALECOCares"

b"Congratulations to Mr. Hernando Barbante and Mr. Ricky Navales for being selected as recipients of the prestigious 2023 Electric Cooperatives' Most Outstanding Lineworker award.\n\nThe awarding ceremony which took place at PENELCO Headquarters in Balanga City, Bataan on October 6, 2023, was organized by the National Electrification Administration (NEA) and led by Deputy Administrator for EC Management, Atty. Omar Mayo. The event intends to recognize and honor the exceptional contributions and roles of our lineworkers in advancing the electrification program in the country.\n\nWe, your ALECO family, are extremely proud of your achievement. b'Sa aming mga Member-Consumer-Owners,\n\xe2\x80\x8b\nNais naming ipaalam na magkakaroon kami ng Disconnection Activity sa ilang lugar. Bilang bahagi ng aming patuloy na pagsusumikap upang matiyak ang patas at mahusay na operasyon, ang mga account na mayroong outstanding bills o arrears ay maaring maputulan.\n\xe2\x80\x8b\nAlinsunod sa aming patakaran at pamamaraan, ang mga account na may outstanding bills o arrears sa loob ng itinalagang takdang panahon ay mapuputulan ng suplay ng kuryente. Ang hakbang na ito ay kinakailangan upang mapanatili ang pinansyal na aspeto ng kooperatiba at mapangalagaan ang interes ng bawat Member-Consumer-Owners.\n\xe2\x80\x8b\nUpang maiwasan ang pagkadiskonekta ng inyong suplay ng kuryente, inirerekomenda naming isaalang-alang ang mga sumusunod na opsyon upang mabayaran ang inyong power bills sa takdang panahon:\n1. \xf0\x9d\x90\x8f\xf0\x9d\x90\x9e\xf0\x9d\x90\xab\xf0\x9d\x90\xac\xf0\x9d\x90\xa8\xf0\x9d\x90\xa7\xf0\x9d\x90\x9a\xf0\x9d\x90\xa5 \xf0\x9d\x90\xa7\xf0\x9d\x90\x9a \xf0\x9d\x90\x8f\xf0\x9d\x90\x9a\xf0\x9d\x90\xa0\xf0\x9d\x90\x9b\xf0\x9d\x90\x9a\xf0\x9d\x90\x9b\xf0\x9d\x90\x9a\xf0\x9d\x90\xb2\xf0\x9d\x90\x9a\xf0\x9d\x90\x9d: Bisitahin ang malapit na ASCO para magbayad. Ang aming mga tauhan ay handang tumulong sa inyo at magbigay ng kinakailangang gabay.\n2. \xf0\x9d\x90\x80\xf0\x9d\x90\x8b\xf0\x9d\x90\x84\xf0\x9d\x90\x82\xf0\x9d\x90\x8e \xf0\x9d\x90\x8f\xf0\x9d\x90\x9a\xf0\x9d\x90\xb2\xf0\x9d\x90\xa6\xf0\x9d\x90\x9e\xf0\x9d\x90\xa7\xf0\x9d\x90\xad \xf0\x9d\x90\x82\xf0\x9d\x90\x9e\xf0\x9d\x90\xa7\xf0\x9d\x90\xad\xf0\x9d\x90\x9e\xf0\x9d\x90\xab\xf0\x9d\x90\xac: Maaring magbayad sa aming mga akreditadong payment centers para sa mabilis na transaksyon.\n\xe2\x80\xa2 Bayad Center\n\xe2\x80\xa2 Camalig Bank\n\xe2\x80\xa2 ECPay\n\xe2\x80\xa2 UnionBank\n\xe2\x80\x8b\nPinapaalala namin na napakahalaga na mabayaran kaagad ang inyong power bills upang maiwasan ang anumang pagkaantala sa inyong suplay ng kuryente. Kapag naputulan, kinakailangan na bayaran ang lahat ng outstanding bills kasama ang bayad para sa pagpapabalik ng serbisyo (reconnection fee).\n\xe2\x80\x8b\nPinahahalagahan namin ang inyong pagiging Member-Consumer-Owners at ang tiwala na inyong ibinigay sa ating kooperatiba. Sa pamamagitan ng pagtutulungan upang mabayaran ang ating power bills sa loob ng takdang panahon, masisiguro natin ang patuloy na maayos at abot-kayang suplay ng kuryente para sa lahat ng mga miyembro ng kooperatiba.\n\xe2\x80\x8b\nMaraming salamat sa inyong atensyon at kooperasyon.\n\xe2\x80\x8b\n\xf0\x9d\x90\x83\xf0\x9d\x90\x84\xf0\x9d\x90\x93\xf0\x9d\x90\x80\xf0\x9d\x90\x88\xf0\x9d\x90\x8b\xf0\x9d\x90\x92 \xf0\x9d\x90\x81\xf0\x9d\x90\x84\xf0\x9d\x90\x8b\xf0\x9d\x90\x8e\xf0\x9d\x90\x96:\xf0\x9f\x94\x8c\n\xe2\x80\x8b\n\xf0\x9d\x90\x83\xf0\x9d\x90\x88\xf0\x9d\x90\x92\xf0\x9d\x90\x82\xf0\x9d\x90\x8e\xf0\x9d\x90\x8d\xf0\x9d\x90\x8d\xf0\x9d\x90\x84\xf0\x9d\x90\x82\xf0\x9d\x90\x93\xf0\x9d\x90\x88\xf0\x9d\x90\x8e\xf0\x9d\x90\x8d \xf0\x9d\x90\x92\xf0\x9d\x90\x82\xf0\x9d\x90\x87\xf0\x9d\x90\x84\xf0\x9d\x90\x83\xf0\x9d\x90\x94\xf0\x9d\x90\x8b\xf0\x9d\x90\x84: OCTOBER 10 - b"Congratulations to the newly elected officers of BAPA Oson, Tabaco!\n\nMembers of BAPA gathered at the Barangay Hall of Barangay Oson, Tabaco for an assembly meeting and election of new set of officers.\n\nDuring the officer election, Mr. Casil, ALECO BAPA Coordinator, engaged in discussions with the newly elected officials about the BAPA Constitution and By-laws, the organization's community objectives, and the roles and responsibilities of BAPA Officers.\n\nAdditionally, Mr. Casil addressed topics such as monthly rate calculations, system loss distribution, and potential strategies in reducing BAPA consumption.\n\n\xf0\x9f\x92\x9b\xf0\x9f\x92\x99"
b'\xf0\x9d\x94\xbb\xf0\x9d\x95\x9a\xf0\x9d\x95\x95 \xf0\x9d\x95\xaa\xf0\x9d\x95\xa0\xf0\x9d\x95\xa6 \xf0\x9d\x95\x9c\xf0\x9d\x95\x9f\xf0\x9d\x95\xa0\xf0\x9d\x95\xa8? \xf0\x9f\x91\x87\n\nElectricity was known to have reached the country in 1890. Sociedad Mercantil which became La Electricista provided electricity in Manila and nearby provinces. La Electricista was established in 1892 in association with the Compania de Tabacos de Filipinas (TABACALERA). \n\nThe Municipal Council of Manila signed a 20-year contract with Sociedad Mercantil Millat, Marti y Mitjans to provide electric lighting for city streets, parks and other public places originally illuminated by oil lamps. The contract also allowed Sociedad to enter into arrangements with private customers to have their homes and establishments lighted by incandescent lamps. \n\nLa Electricista was given rights to Sociedad\xe2\x80\x99s 20-year contract. MERALCO was established in 1903 and bought La Electricista the following year. By early 1905, some 40,129 incandescent lights, 495 arc lamps were installed in both public and private areas (Cabrera, 1992).\n\nReferences: https://tinyurl.com/2p8zp2vv\n\n#ALECOknows'
b'"Disasters happen. How we prepare for them is what makes the difference." - Robert D. Bullard \n\nOn October 5, 2023, ALECO management organized fire and earthquake drills within the ALECO compound. With speakers from the Bureau of Fire Protection (BFP) - Legazpi City Fire Station, the participants actively engaged in the activities and executed the necessary protocols as demonstrated in the lectures. The objective of the drill was to enhance safety and readiness for individuals and communities in case of emergencies. \n\nTruly, through adequate training and safety preparedness and guidance on the correct procedures to follow during emergencies, panic and anxiety will be minimized among our workforce during real emergency scenarios. \n\nThank you very much to our hero firefighters in the BFP for equipping us with a clear understanding of our roles and responsibilities in order for us to promote a well-coordinated and organized response in crisis situations.\n\nMabalos po!\n\n\xf0\x9f\x92\x9b\xf0\x9f\x92\x99'

b'Sa aming mga Member-Consumer-Owners,\n\xe2\x80\x8b\nNais naming ipaalam na magkakaroon kami ng Disconnection Activity sa ilang lugar. Bilang bahagi ng aming patuloy na pagsusumikap upang matiyak ang patas at mahusay na operasyon, ang mga account na mayroong outstanding bills o arrears ay maaring maputulan.\n\xe2\x80\x8b\nAlinsunod sa aming patakaran at pamamaraan, ang mga account na may outstanding bills o arrears sa loob ng itinalagang takdang panahon ay mapuputulan ng suplay ng kuryente. Ang hakbang na ito ay kinakailangan upang mapanatili ang pinansyal na aspeto ng kooperatiba at mapangalagaan ang interes ng bawat Member-Consumer-Owners.\n\xe2\x80\x8b\nUpang maiwasan ang pagkadiskonekta ng inyong suplay ng kuryente, inirerekomenda naming isaalang-alang ang mga sumusunod na opsyon upang mabayaran ang inyong power bills sa takdang panahon:\n1. \xf0\x9d\x90\x8f\xf0\x9d\x90\x9e\xf0\x9d\x90\xab\xf0\x9d\x90\xac\xf0\x9d\x90\xa8\xf0\x9d\x90\xa7\xf0\x9d\x90\x9a\xf0\x9d\x90\xa5 \xf0\x9d\x90\xa7\xf0\x9d\x90\x9a \xf0\x9d\x90\x8f\xf0\x9d\x90\x9a\xf0\x9d\x90\xa0\xf0\x9d\x90\x9b\xf0\x9d\x90\x9a\xf0\x9d\x90\x9b\xf0\x9d\x90\x9a\xf0\x9d\x90\xb2\xf0\x9d\x90\x9a\xf0\x9d\x90\x9d: Bisitahin ang malapit na ASCO para magbayad. Ang aming mga tauhan ay handang tumulong sa inyo at magbigay ng kinakailangang gabay.\n2. \xf0\x9d\x90\x80\xf0\x9d\x90\x8b\xf0\x9d\x90\x84\xf0\x9d\x90\x82\xf0\x9d\x90\x8e \xf0\x9d\x90\x8f\xf0\x9d\x90\x9a\xf0\x9d\x90\xb2\xf0\x9d\x90\xa6\xf0\x9d\x90\x9e\xf0\x9d\x90\xa7\xf0\x9d\x90\xad \xf0\x9d\x90\x82\xf0\x9d\x90\x9e\xf0\x9d\x90\xa7\xf0\x9d\x90\xad\xf0\x9d\x90\x9e\xf0\x9d\x90\xab\xf0\x9d\x90\xac: Maaring magbayad sa aming mga akreditadong payment centers para sa mabilis na transaksyon.\n\xe2\x80\xa2 Bayad Center\n\xe2\x80\xa2 Camalig Bank\n\xe2\x80\xa2 ECPay\n\xe2\x80\xa2 UnionBank\n\xe2\x80\x8b\nPinapaalala namin na napakahalaga na mabayaran kaagad ang inyong power bills upang maiwasan ang anumang pagkaantala sa inyong suplay ng kuryente. Kapag naputulan, kinakailangan na bayaran ang lahat ng outstanding bills kasama ang bayad para sa pagpapabalik ng serbisyo (reconnection fee).\n\xe2\x80\x8b\nPinahahalagahan namin ang inyong pagiging Member-Consumer-Owners at ang tiwala na inyong ibinigay sa ating kooperatiba. Sa pamamagitan ng pagtutulungan upang mabayaran ang ating power bills sa loob ng takdang panahon, masisiguro natin ang patuloy na maayos at abot-kayang suplay ng kuryente para sa lahat ng mga miyembro ng kooperatiba.\n\xe2\x80\x8b\nMaraming salamat sa inyong atensyon at kooperasyon.\n\xe2\x80\x8b\n\xf0\x9d\x90\x83\xf0\x9d\x90\x84\xf0\x9d\x90\x93\xf0\x9d\x90\x80\xf0\x9d\x90\x88\xf0\x9d\x90\x8b\xf0\x9d\x90\x92 \xf0\x9d\x90\x81\xf0\x9d\x90\x84\xf0\x9d\x90\x8b\xf0\x9d\x90\x8e\xf0\x9d\x90\x96:\xf0\x9f\x94\x8c\n\xe2\x80\x8b\n\xf0\x9d\x90\x83\xf0\x9d\x90\x88\xf0\x9d\x90\x92\xf0\x9d\x90\x82\xf0\x9d\x90\x8e\xf0\x9d\x90\x8d\xf0\x9d\x90\x8d\xf0\x9d\x90\x84\xf0\x9d\x90\x82\xf0\x9d\x90\x93\xf0\x9d\x90\x88\xf0\x9d\x90\x8e\xf0\x9d\x90\x8d \xf0\x9d\x90\x92\xf0\x9d\x90\x82\xf0\x9d\x90\x87\xf0\x9d\x90\x84\xf0\x9d\x90\x83\xf0\x9d\x90\x94\xf0\x9d\x90\x8b\xf0\x9d\x90\x84: OCTOBER 3 - b'This October, we observe National Cooperative Month!\n\nEmbracing the 2023 theme, "Pioneering the Path to Recovery Amidst Modern Challenges of Climate Change and Food Security," we recognize and extend our appreciation for the valuable contributions of cooperatives within our society.\n\nCooperatives serve as crucial entities in managing both environmental sustainability and food production. Faced with the obstacles presented by climate change, cooperatives are instrumental in supporting our society, particularly the agricultural sector. By harnessing our collective capabilities, which encompass knowledge sharing and training, research and innovation, as well as resource pooling and collective action, we are able to provide the resources needed by our community.\n\n#albayelectriccooperative\n#NationalCooperativeMonth\n#CooperativeMonth2023'

b'Sa aming mga Member-Consumer-Owners,\n\xe2\x80\x8b\nNais naming ipaalam na magkakaroon kami ng Disconnection Activity sa ilang lugar. Bilang bahagi ng aming patuloy na pagsusumikap upang matiyak ang patas at mahusay na operasyon, ang mga account na mayroong outstanding bills o arrears ay maaring maputulan.\n\xe2\x80\x8b\nAlinsunod sa aming patakaran at pamamaraan, ang mga account na may outstanding bills o arrears sa loob ng itinalagang takdang panahon ay mapuputulan ng suplay ng kuryente. Ang hakbang na ito ay kinakailangan upang mapanatili ang pinansyal na aspeto ng kooperatiba at mapangalagaan ang interes ng bawat Member-Consumer-Owners.\n\xe2\x80\x8b\nUpang maiwasan ang pagkadiskonekta ng inyong suplay ng kuryente, inirerekomenda naming isaalang-alang ang mga sumusunod na opsyon upang mabayaran ang inyong power bills sa takdang panahon:\n1. \xf0\x9d\x90\x8f\xf0\x9d\x90\x9e\xf0\x9d\x90\xab\xf0\x9d\x90\xac\xf0\x9d\x90\xa8\xf0\x9d\x90\xa7\xf0\x9d\x90\x9a\xf0\x9d\x90\xa5 \xf0\x9d\x90\xa7\xf0\x9d\x90\x9a \xf0\x9d\x90\x8f\xf0\x9d\x90\x9a\xf0\x9d\x90\xa0\xf0\x9d\x90\x9b\xf0\x9d\x90\x9a\xf0\x9d\x90\x9b\xf0\x9d\x90\x9a\xf0\x9d\x90\xb2\xf0\x9d\x90\x9a\xf0\x9d\x90\x9d: Bisitahin ang malapit na ASCO para magbayad. Ang aming mga tauhan ay handang tumulong sa inyo at magbigay ng kinakailangang gabay.\n2. \xf0\x9d\x90\x80\xf0\x9d\x90\x8b\xf0\x9d\x90\x84\xf0\x9d\x90\x82\xf0\x9d\x90\x8e \xf0\x9d\x90\x8f\xf0\x9d\x90\x9a\xf0\x9d\x90\xb2\xf0\x9d\x90\xa6\xf0\x9d\x90\x9e\xf0\x9d\x90\xa7\xf0\x9d\x90\xad \xf0\x9d\x90\x82\xf0\x9d\x90\x9e\xf0\x9d\x90\xa7\xf0\x9d\x90\xad\xf0\x9d\x90\x9e\xf0\x9d\x90\xab\xf0\x9d\x90\xac: Maaring magbayad sa aming mga akreditadong payment centers para sa mabilis na transaksyon.\n\xe2\x80\xa2 Bayad Center\n\xe2\x80\xa2 Camalig Bank\n\xe2\x80\xa2 ECPay\n\xe2\x80\xa2 UnionBank\n\xe2\x80\x8b\nPinapaalala namin na napakahalaga na mabayaran kaagad ang inyong power bills upang maiwasan ang anumang pagkaantala sa inyong suplay ng kuryente. Kapag naputulan, kinakailangan na bayaran ang lahat ng outstanding bills kasama ang bayad para sa pagpapabalik ng serbisyo (reconnection fee).\n\xe2\x80\x8b\nPinahahalagahan namin ang inyong pagiging Member-Consumer-Owners at ang tiwala na inyong ibinigay sa ating kooperatiba. Sa pamamagitan ng pagtutulungan upang mabayaran ang ating power bills sa loob ng takdang panahon, masisiguro natin ang patuloy na maayos at abot-kayang suplay ng kuryente para sa lahat ng mga miyembro ng kooperatiba.\n\xe2\x80\x8b\nMaraming salamat sa inyong atensyon at kooperasyon.\n\xe2\x80\x8b\n\xf0\x9d\x90\x83\xf0\x9d\x90\x84\xf0\x9d\x90\x93\xf0\x9d\x90\x80\xf0\x9d\x90\x88\xf0\x9d\x90\x8b\xf0\x9d\x90\x92 \xf0\x9d\x90\x81\xf0\x9d\x90\x84\xf0\x9d\x90\x8b\xf0\x9d\x90\x8e\xf0\x9d\x90\x96:\xf0\x9f\x94\x8c\n\xe2\x80\x8b\n\xf0\x9d\x90\x83\xf0\x9d\x90\x88\xf0\x9d\x90\x92\xf0\x9d\x90\x82\xf0\x9d\x90\x8e\xf0\x9d\x90\x8d\xf0\x9d\x90\x8d\xf0\x9d\x90\x84\xf0\x9d\x90\x82\xf0\x9d\x90\x93\xf0\x9d\x90\x88\xf0\x9d\x90\x8e\xf0\x9d\x90\x8d \xf0\x9d\x90\x92\xf0\x9d\x90\x82\xf0\x9d\x90\x87\xf0\x9d\x90\x84\xf0\x9d\x90\x83\xf0\x9d\x90\x94\xf0\x9d\x90\x8b\xf0\x9d\x90\x84: SEPTEMBER 26 - 29 (TUESDAY - FRIDAY)\n\xe2\x80\x8b\n\xf0\x9d\x90\x92\xf0\x9d\x90\x84\xf0\x9d\x90\x8f\xf0\x9d\x90\x93\xf0\x9d\x90\x84\xf0\x9d\x90\x8c\xf0\x9d\x90\x81\xf0\x9d\x90\x84\xf0\x9d\x90\x91 \xf0\x9d\x9f\x90\xf0\x9d\x9f\x94\n   Daraga\n   Legazpi\n   Libon\n   Ligao\n   Malinao\n   Tabaco\n\n\xf0\x9d\x90\x92\xf0\x9d\x90\x84\xf0\x9d\x90\x8f\xf0\x9d\x90\x93\xf0\x9d\x90\x84\xf0\x9d\x90\x8c\xf0\x9d\x90\x81\xf0\x9d\x90\x84\xf0\x9d\x90\x91 \xf0\x9d\x9f\x90\xf0\x9d\x9f\x95\n   Bacacay\n   Daraga\n   Legazpi\n   Ligao\n   Polangui\n   Tabaco\n\n\xf0\x9d\x90\x92\xf0\x9d\x90\x84\xf0\x9d\x90\x8f\xf0\x9d\x90\x93\xf0\x9d\x90\x84\xf0\x9d\x90\x8c\xf0\x9d\x90\x81\xf0\x9d\x90\x84\xf0\x9d\x90\x91 \xf0\x9d\x9f\x90\xf0\x9d\x9f\x96\n   Guinobatan\n   Legazpi\n   Oas\n   Sto. b'Bukas, ika-13 ng Setyembre 2023, mula alas-8 ng umaga hanggang alas-5 ng hapon, magkakaroon ng massive right-of-way line clearing sa ilang mga barangay na sakop ng Ligao Feeder 1. Massive right of way line clearing'
b'Nais naming ipaalam sa aming mga Member-Consumer-Owners na ang aming Globe hotline na may numero na \xf0\x9d\x9f\x8e\xf0\x9d\x9f\x97\xf0\x9d\x9f\x97\xf0\x9d\x9f\x93-\xf0\x9d\x9f\x95\xf0\x9d\x9f\x90\xf0\x9d\x9f\x97\xf0\x9d\x9f\x94-\xf0\x9d\x9f\x91\xf0\x9d\x9f\x91\xf0\x9d\x9f\x90 ay hindi na magagamit. Ito ay biglaang hindi na makatanggap ng anumang tawag o mensahe. Gayunpaman, maaari kayong makipag-ugnayan sa aming bagong hotline (Smart) na may numerong \xf0\x9d\x9f\x8e\xf0\x9d\x9f\x97\xf0\x9d\x9f\x90\xf0\x9d\x9f\x97-\xf0\x9d\x9f\x90\xf0\x9d\x9f\x94\xf0\x9d\x9f\x96\xf0\x9d\x9f\x91-\xf0\x9d\x9f\x97\xf0\x9d\x9f\x8e\xf0\x9d\x9f\x92 para sa inyong mga concerns. \n\nMaraming salamat, ka-ALECO!'

Filipino citizen, 21 to 70 years old on the date of election;\n\n2. Actual resident and member-consumer of the district for the past two (2) years;\n\n3. Bachelor\xe2\x80\x99s degree holder;\n\n4. Has attended at least two (2) annual general membership assembly for the last five (5) years;\n\n5. Member of good standing\n a. Incumbent member of the ALECO Board of Directors seeking re-election - Unsettled or outstanding obligations include power bills, cash advances, disallowances (including NEA audit findings) and materials and equipment issuances;\n c. Has not been apprehended of electric pilferage;\n\n7. Has not been convicted of a crime involving moral turpitude, or terminated from public office or government / private employee for just cause;\n\n8. Has not been employed by or has financial interest in a competing enterprise or business selling electric energy, electrical hardware or transactions which in any way affect the management and operation of ALECO;\n\n9. Such person or his or her spouse was not a candidate in the recent local or national election nor hold an elective / appointive position with Salary Grade of 16 and above; and\n\n10. Such person is not related within the fourth civil degree of consanguinity or affinity to any member of ALECO Board of Directors, Department Manager, Acting General Manager or Project Supervisor.'

Ang mga baranggay na apektado ng aktibidad na ito ay ang mga sumusunod: (Portion) Sagmin, Ba\xc3\xb1o, Bagumbayan, Ilawod West, Ilawod Poblacion, Kawit-East Washington Drive, Rizal St., Ilawod, Ilawod, Cruzada.\n\n\xf0\x9d\x90\x83\xf0\x9d\x90\x84\xf0\x9d\x90\x93\xf0\x9d\x90\x80\xf0\x9d\x90\x88\xf0\x9d\x90\x8b\xf0\x9d\x90\x92 \xf0\x9d\x90\x81\xf0\x9d\x90\x84\xf0\x9d\x90\x8b\xf0\x9d\x90\x8e\xf0\x9d\x90\x96: \xf0\x9f\x91\x87 \xf0\x9f\x91\x87 \xf0\x9f\x91\x87\n\xf0\x9d\x90\x92\xf0\x9d\x90\x82\xf0\x9d\x90\x87\xf0\x9d\x90\x84\xf0\x9d\x90\x83\xf0\x9d\x90\x94\xf0\x9d\x90\x8b\xf0\x9d\x90\x84\xf0\x9d\x90\x83 \xf0\x9d\x90\x8f\xf0\x9d\x90\x8e\xf0\x9d\x97\xaa\xf0\x9d\x90\x84\xf0\x9d\x90\x91 \xf0\x9d\x90\x88\xf0\x9d\x90\x8d\xf0\x9d\x90\x93\xf0\x9d\x90\x84\xf0\x9d\x90\x91\xf0\x9d\x90\x91\xf0\x9d\x90\x94\xf0\x9d\x90\x8f\xf0\x9d\x90\x93\xf0\x9d\x90\x88\xf0\x9d\x90\x8e\xf0\x9d\x90\x8d\n\xf0\x9d\x90\x83\xf0\x9d\x90\x80\xf0\x9d\x90\x93\xf0\x9d\x90\x84: AUGUST 31, 2023\n\xf0\x9d\x90\x83\xf0\x9d\x90\x94\xf0\x9d\x90\x91\xf0\x9d\x90\x80\xf0\x9d\x90\x93\xf0\x9d\x90\x88\xf0\x9d\x90\x8e\xf0\x9d\x90\x8d: 8:00 AM - 5:00 PM\n\xf0\x9d\x90\x92\xf0\x9d\x90\x94\xf0\x9d\x90\x81\xf0\x9d\x90\x92\xf0\x9d\x90\x93\xf0\x9d\x90\x80\xf0\x9d\x90\x93\xf0\x9d\x90\x88\xf0\x9d\x90\x8e\xf0\x9d\x90\x8d: WASHINGTON FEEDER 1\n\xf0\x9d\x90\x80\xf0\x9d\x90\x85\xf0\x9d\x90\x85\xf0\x9d\x90\x84\xf0\x9d\x90\x82\xf0\x9d\x90\x93\xf0\x9d\x90\x84\xf0\x9d\x90\x83 \xf0\x9d\x90\x80\xf0\x9d\x90\x91\xf0\x9d\x90\x84\xf0\x9d\x90\x80\xf0\x9d\x90\x92: (Portion) Sagmin, Ba\xc3\xb1o, Bagumbayan, Ilawod West, Ilawod Poblacion, Kawit-East Washington Drive, Rizal St., Ilawod, Ilawod, Cruzada\n\xf0\x9d\x90\x91\xf0\x9d\x90\x84\xf0\x9d\x90\x80\xf0\x9d\x90\x92\xf0\x9d\x90\x8e\xf0\x9d\x90\x8d: Massive Vegetation Line Clearing / Replacement of Poles'
b'\xf0\x9d\x90\x8d\xf0\x9d\x90\x8e\xf0\x9d\x90\x93\xf0\x9d\x90\x88\xf0\x9d\x90\x82\xf0\x9d\x90\x84 \xf0\x9d\x90\x8e\xf0\x9d\x90\x85 \xf0\x9d\x90\x84\xf0\x9d\x90\x8c\xf0\x9d\x90\x84\xf0\x9d\x90\x91\xf0\x9d\x90\x86\xf0\x9d\x90\x84\xf0\x9d\x90\x8d\xf0\x9d\x90\x82\xf0\x9d\x90\x98 \xf0\x9d\x90\x8f\xf0\x9d\x90\x8e\xf0\x9d\x90\x96\xf0\x9d\x90\x84\xf0\x9d\x90\x91 \xf0\x9d\x90\x88\xf0\x9d\x90\x8d\xf0\x9d\x90\x93\xf0\x9d\x90\x84\xf0\x9d\x90\x91\xf0\x9d\x90\x91\xf0\x9d\x90\x94\xf0\x9d\x90\x8f\xf0\x9d\x90\x93\xf0\x9d\x90\x88\xf0\x9d\x90\x8e\xf0\x9d\x90\x8d\n\n\xf0\x9d\x90\x92\xf0\x9d\x90\x94\xf0\x9d\x90\x81\xf0\x9d\x90\x92\xf0\x9d\x90\x93\xf0\x9d\x90\x80\xf0\x9d\x90\x93\xf0\x9d\x90\x88\xf0\x9d\x90\x8e\xf0\x9d\x90\x8d: WASHINGTON FEEDER 2\n\xf0\x9d\x90\x93\xf0\x9d\x90\x88\xf0\x9d\x90\x8c\xf0\x9d\x90\x84 \xf0\x9d\x90\x83\xf0\x9d\x90\x94\xf0\x9d\x90\x91\xf0\x9d\x90\x80\xf0\x9d\x90\x93\xf0\x9d\x90\x88\xf0\x9d\x90\x8e\xf0\x9d\x90\x8d: 8:00 AM - 5:00 PM (8hrs)\n\xf0\x9d\x90\x80\xf0\x9d\x90\x85\xf0\x9d\x90\x85\xf0\x9d\x90\x84\xf0\x9d\x90\x82\xf0\x9d\x90\x93\xf0\x9d\x90\x84\xf0\x9d\x90\x83 \xf0\x9d\x90\x80\xf0\x9d\x90\x91\xf0\x9d\x90\x84\xf0\x9d\x90\x80\xf0\x9d\x90\x92: \n (Lateral going to Sto. Cristo and San Roque Daraga, Albay)\n\xf0\x9d\x90\x91\xf0\x9d\x90\x84\xf0\x9d\x90\x80\xf0\x9d\x90\x92\xf0\x9d\x90\x8e\xf0\x9d\x90\x8d: Replacement of pole \n\xf0\x9d\x90\x83\xf0\x9d\x90\x80\xf0\x9d\x90\x93\xf0\x9d\x90\x84: August 30, 2023'
b'Sa ika-30 ng Agosto 2023, isasagawa ang pag-relocate ng lateral na makakaapekto sa bahagi ng P2, Barangay 17, Rizal Street, Legazpi City mula alas-12 ng hating gabi hanggang alas-8 ng umaga.\n\nUpang maisakatuparan ang aktibidad na ito, magkakaroon ng pag-isolate ng linya mula alas-12 ng hating gabi hanggang ala-1 ng madaling araw at mula ala-7 hanggang alas-8 ng umaga. b'Philippine Rural Electric Cooperatives Association\n\nPanalangin para sa Electric Cooperative\n\nMahal na Panginoon,\n\nSa panahon pong matindi ang pagsubok, hindi kayo nagkulang sa pagbibigay sa amin ng lakas, tibay ng loob, at inspirasyon upang malampasan ang lahat ng bagay. Sa dami po nang naganap at magaganap pa, alam po naming hindi Niyo kami pababayaan na mag-isa sa landas na gusto ninyo para sa amin. Taos puso po ang aming pagpapasalamat sa lakas ng loob na ibinigay ninyo nitong mga nakaraang buwan upang malampasan namin ang lahat ng pagsubok.\n\nPanginoon, sa ngayon pong maraming bagay ang sumusubok sa katatagan ng aming samahan, sana po ay bigyan niyo kami ng klarong pag-iisip upang makita namin ang rason at perspektibo ninyo sa lahat ng pinagdaraanan namin. Sana po ay magkaroon ng linaw ang lahat sa tulong ninyo.\n\nKayo lamang po ang nakakaalam ng mga paraan at daan para sa ikabubuti ng bawat isa, kaya po sa inyo namin ibinibigay ang lahat ng tiwala at pananalig.\n\nHiling namin na tulungan po ninyo ang mga lider ng bansa upang makagawa sila ng mga desisyong makakabuti para sa lahat.\nNgayon pong maraming pagsubok ang bansa, sana po ay mabigyang halaga ng bawat lider ng bansa ang tunay na dahilan kung bakit sila nailagay sa kanilang mga posisyon. Sana po ay gamitin nila ang kanilang mga kakayanan upang makatulong sa iba at sa bansa, at hindi para sa pansariling kapakanan at interes.\n\nGabayan din po ninyo ang bawat lider at manggagawa ng sektor ng Rural Electrification upang maging malakas, matatag, at mapagmahal sa tungkulin at aming adbokasiya. Bigyan niyo po ang bawat isa ng malusog na pangangatawan upang magampanan nila ang kanilang mga trabaho at tungkulin.\n\nPanginoon, lalo niyo pa po sanang gabayan ang lahat ng electric cooperatives na walang ibang hangad kundi ang magbigay ng serbisyong dekalidad para sa mga member-consumer-owners. Patatagin at gabayan niyo po lalo ang BENECO at mga electric cooperatives sa Negros Island upang lampasan ang kahit anong hirap o pagsubok na kanilang pagdaraanan.\n\nPatatagin po ninyo ang NORDECO na kasalukuyang nakararanas ng panggigipit mula sa mga malalaking korporasyon at maiimpluwensiyang tao sa lipunan na nagnanais kunin at sakupin ang pamamahala sa nasabing kooperatiba para sa mga makasariling layunin, pansariling kitang-pinansyal, at mga layuning hindi makabubuti sa aming mga member-consumer-owners. Bigyan mo po ng kalinawan ng pag-iisip ang mga kontra-kooperatibang grupo na ito, kasama na ang mga member-consumer-owners na pilit nilang pinapaniwala sa mga maling impormasyon.\n\nHinihingi din namin ang inyong gabay para sa CASURECO III at lahat ng mga electric cooperatives namin sa Bicol lalo pa\xe2\x80\x99t sila rin ay may kinahaharap na pagsubok. Huwag niyo po sanang hayaang makuha ng ibang korporasyon ang pagbibigay serbisyo sa aming mga MCOs sa Bicol sapagkat ang layunin nila ay taliwas sa ikabubuti ng lahat.\n\nAmin rin pong itinataas sa inyo ang mga pagsubok na kinahaharap ng ILECO I. Naway ito ay malampasan ng mga empleyado, lider, at pati na rin po ng mga MCOs.\n\nSana po ay haplusin ninyo ng inyong pagmamahal ang mga puso ng mga taong pansarili lamang ang tunay na hangad. Baguhin sana ninyo ang direksyon ng kanilang buhay upang makita nila ang pagmamahal ninyo sa kanila.\n\nLahat po ng kritisismo ay naway magbigay sa amin ng mas maayos na direksyon at magbigay samin ng lakas upang lalo pang maging matibay. Sa tulong ninyo, naway humina po ang mga pwersang hindi magreresulta sa kasaganaan at kaayusan ng mga MCOs at ng bayan.\n\nProtektahan niyo po ang lahat ng electric cooperatives sa mga taong hindi maganda ang hangarin para sa iba. Inaangat namin ang lahat sa inyo at sana po ay patuloy niyo pong maipakita sa amin a\n\nSa lahat ng ito Panginoon, patuloy naming itinataas sa inyo ang lahat na aming takot at pangamba. Patuloy niyo po kaming gawing instrumento ng inyong kabutihan.\n\nAmen.\n\n#ECBlackFridayProtest\n#HandsOffOurECsNoToTakeOver\n#ECIndependenceWeWillNotBeSilenced\n#UnitedWeStandWeStandUnitedforBENECO\n#UnitedWeStandWeStandUnitedforCASURECOIIIandAllECsinBicol\n#UnitedWeStandWeStandUnitedforILECOI\n#UnitedWeStandWeStandUnitedforNORDECO\n#UnitedWeStandWeStandUnitedforAllECsInNegrosIsland'
